<h1 id="user-content-setting-up-the-aws-eks-provisioning-workflow-on-github" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-setting-up-the-aws-eks-provisioning-workflow-on-github" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#setting-up-the-aws-eks-provisioning-workflow-on-github"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Setting up the AWS EKS provisioning workflow on GitHub</h1>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">In this section we will create a workflow which will provision an AWS EKS cluster. This workflow will be configured to be manually triggered by the user. As part of EKS cluster provisioning, a NGINX Ingress controller is deployed and a .env file with the name <code>eks-variables</code> is created in .github folder, which contains, among others, the DNS name of the Ingress controller, that you you will need to add as CNAME record on the domains used in your application Ingress manifest files. Refer to the appendix to retrieve the DNS name of the Ingress controller independently.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The creation of the workflow will follow the project workflow, so a new branch named <code>feature/eks-provisioning</code> will be created, the YAML file for the workflow and the terraform files for creating the cluster will be pushed to it.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Then, a Pull Request (PR) will be created in order to merge the new branch into the appropriate branch (provided in <code>-b</code> flag). The PR will be automatically merged if the repository policies are met. If the merge is not possible, either the PR URL will be shown as output, or it will be opened in your web browser if using <code>-w</code> flag.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The script located at <code>/scripts/pipelines/github/pipeline_generator.sh</code> will automatically create this new branch, create the EKS provisioning workflow based on the YAML template, create the Pull Request and, if it is possible, merge this new branch into the specified branch.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-prerequisites" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prerequisites</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Add AWS credentials as <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/actions/security-guides/encrypted-secrets#creating-encrypted-secrets-for-a-repository">Github Secrets</a> in your repository.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A S3 Bucket. You can use an existing one or <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/cli/latest/userguide/cli-services-s3-commands.html#using-s3-commands-managing-buckets-creating" rel="nofollow">create a new one</a> with the following command:</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="aws s3 mb &lt;bucket name&gt;
# Example: aws s3 mb s3://terraformStateBucket"><pre class="notranslate"><code>aws s3 mb &lt;bucket name&gt;
# Example: aws s3 mb s3://terraformStateBucket</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">An AWS IAM user with <a href="https://github.com/devonfw/hangar/blob/master/documentation/aws/setup-aws-account-iam-for-eks.asciidoc#check-iam-user-permissions">required permissions</a> to provision the EKS cluster.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">This script will commit and push the corresponding YAML template into your repository, so please be sure your local repository is up-to-date (i.e you have pulled the latest changes with <code>git pull</code>).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Creating the workflow using provided script</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Before executing the workflow generator, you will need to customize some input variables about the environment. Also, you may want to use existing VPC and subnets instead of creating new ones. To do so, you can either edit <code>terraform.tfvars</code> file or take advantage of the <code>set-terraform-variables.sh</code> script located at <code>/scripts/environment-provisioning/aws/eks</code>, which allows you to create or update values for the required variables, passing them as flags.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Example: creating a new VPC on cluster creation:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./set-terraform-variables.sh --region &lt;region name&gt; --instance_type &lt;workers instance type&gt; --vpc_name &lt;vpc name&gt; --vpc_cidr_block &lt;vpc cidr block&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./set-terraform-variables.sh --region &lt;region name&gt; --instance_type &lt;workers instance type&gt; --vpc_name &lt;vpc name&gt; --vpc_cidr_block &lt;vpc cidr block&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Example: reusing existing VPC and subnets:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./set-terraform-variables.sh --region &lt;region name&gt; --instance_type &lt;workers instance type&gt; --existing_vpc_id &lt;vpc id&gt; --existing_vpc_private_subnets &lt;array of subnet ids&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./set-terraform-variables.sh --region &lt;region name&gt; --instance_type &lt;workers instance type&gt; --existing_vpc_id &lt;vpc id&gt; --existing_vpc_private_subnets &lt;array of subnet ids&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Rancher is installed by default on the cluster after provisioning. If you wish to change this, please update <code>eks-pipeline.cfg</code> accordingly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-usage" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Usage</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pipeline_generator.sh \
  -c &lt;config file path&gt; \
  -n &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  -d &lt;project local path&gt; \
  --cluster-name &lt;cluster name&gt; \
  --s3-bucket &lt;s3 bucket name&gt; \
  --s3-key-path &lt;s3 key path&gt; \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]"><pre class="notranslate"><code>pipeline_generator.sh \
  -c &lt;config file path&gt; \
  -n &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  -d &lt;project local path&gt; \
  --cluster-name &lt;cluster name&gt; \
  --s3-bucket &lt;s3 bucket name&gt; \
  --s3-key-path &lt;s3 key path&gt; \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<table>
<tbody><tr>
<td>
<div dir="auto">Note</div>
</td>
<td>
The config file for the EKS provisioning workflow is located at <code>/scripts/pipelines/github/templates/eks/eks-pipeline.cfg</code>.
</td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-flags" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-flags" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#flags"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Flags</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="-c, --config-file        [Required] Configuration file containing workflow definition.
-n, --pipeline-name      [Required] Name that will be set to the workflow.
-d, --local-directory    [Required] Local directory of your project (the path should always be using '/' and not '\').
    --cluster-name       [Required] Name for the cluster.&quot;
    --s3-bucket          [Required] Name of the S3 bucket where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
    --s3-key-path        [Required] Path within the S3 bucket where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
-b, --target-branch                 Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                  Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag."><pre class="notranslate"><code>-c, --config-file        [Required] Configuration file containing workflow definition.
-n, --pipeline-name      [Required] Name that will be set to the workflow.
-d, --local-directory    [Required] Local directory of your project (the path should always be using '/' and not '\').
    --cluster-name       [Required] Name for the cluster."
    --s3-bucket          [Required] Name of the S3 bucket where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
    --s3-key-path        [Required] Path within the S3 bucket where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
-b, --target-branch                 Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                  Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag.</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-example" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-example" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Example</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./pipeline_generator.sh -c ./templates/eks/eks-pipeline.cfg -n eks-provisioning -d C:/Users/$USERNAME/Desktop/quarkus-project --cluster-name hangar-eks-cluster --s3-bucket terraformStateBucket --s3-key-path eks/state -b develop -w"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./pipeline_generator.sh -c ./templates/eks/eks-pipeline.cfg -n eks-provisioning -d C:/Users/$USERNAME/Desktop/quarkus-project --cluster-name hangar-eks-cluster --s3-bucket terraformStateBucket --s3-key-path eks/state -b develop -w</code></pre></div>
</div>

</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Appendix: Interacting with the cluster</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">First, generate a <code>kubeconfig</code> file for accessing the AWS EKS cluster:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="aws eks update-kubeconfig --name &lt;cluster name&gt; --region &lt;aws region&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>aws eks update-kubeconfig --name &lt;cluster name&gt; --region &lt;aws region&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Now you can use <code>kubectl</code> tool to communicate with the cluster.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">To enable an IAM user to connect to the EKS cluster, please refer <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/eks/latest/userguide/add-user-role.html" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">To get the DNS name of the NGINX Ingress controller on the EKS cluster, run the below command:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="kubectl get svc --namespace nginx-ingress nginx-ingress-nginx-ingress-controller -o jsonpath={.status.loadBalancer.ingress[0].hostname}"><pre class="notranslate"><code>kubectl get svc --namespace nginx-ingress nginx-ingress-nginx-ingress-controller -o jsonpath={.status.loadBalancer.ingress[0].hostname}</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Rancher will be available on <code><a href="https://&lt;ingress" rel="nofollow">https://&lt;ingress</a> controller domain&gt;/dashboard</code>.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-appendix-rancher-resources" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-appendix-rancher-resources" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#appendix-rancher-resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Appendix: Rancher resources</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rancher.com/docs/rancher/v2.6/en/cluster-admin/cluster-access/kubectl/" rel="nofollow">Downloading <code>kubeconfig</code></a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rancher.com/docs/rancher/v2.6/en/admin-settings/rbac/" rel="nofollow">RBAC</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rancher.com/docs/rancher/v2.6/en/monitoring-alerting/" rel="nofollow">Monitoring</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rancher.com/docs/rancher/v2.6/en/logging/" rel="nofollow">Logging</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-setting-up-a-azure-aks-provisioning-workflow-on-github" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#setting-up-a-azure-aks-provisioning-workflow-on-github"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Setting up a Azure AKS provisioning workflow on Github</h1>
<div id="user-content-preamble" dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">In this section we will create a workflow which will provision an Azure AKS cluster. This workflow will be configured to be manually triggered by the user. As part of AKS cluster provisioning, a NGINX Ingress controller is deployed and a variable group with the name <code>aks-variables</code> is created, which contains, among others, the DNS name of the Ingress controller, that you you will need to add as CNAME record on the domains used in your application Ingress manifest files. Refer to the appendix for more details.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The creation of the workflow will follow the project workflow, so a new branch named <code>feature/aks-provisioning</code> will be created, the YAML file for the workflow and the terraform files for creating the cluster will be pushed to it.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Then, a Pull Request (PR) will be created in order to merge the new branch into the appropiate branch (provided in <code>-b</code> flag). The PR will be automatically merged if the repository policies are met. If the merge is not possible, either the PR URL will be shown as output, or it will be opened in your web browser if using <code>-w</code> flag.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The script located at <code>/scripts/pipelines/github/pipeline_generator.sh</code> will automatically create this new branch, create the AKS provisioning workflow based on the YAML template, create the Pull Request and, if it is possible, merge this new branch into the specified branch.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-prerequisites" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prerequisites</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Add AZURE credentials as <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/actions/security-guides/encrypted-secrets#creating-encrypted-secrets-for-a-repository">Github Secrets</a> in your repository and name it <code>AZURE_USERNAME</code>, <code>AZURE_PASSWORD</code>. If you already have a available credentials or you need a specific credentials connection, please update <code>aks-provisioning.yml</code> accordingly.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">An Azure resource group in the desired cluster location (e.g. <code>westeurope</code>). You can use an existing one or create a new one with the following command:</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="az group create -n &lt;resource group name&gt; -l &lt;location&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>az group create -n &lt;resource group name&gt; -l &lt;location&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">An Azure storage account within the previous resource group. You can use an existing one or create a new one with the following command:</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="az storage account create -n &lt;storage account name&gt; -g &lt;resource group name&gt; -l &lt;location&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>az storage account create -n &lt;storage account name&gt; -g &lt;resource group name&gt; -l &lt;location&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">An Azure storage container in Azure within the previous storage account. You can use an existing one or create a new one with the following command:</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="az storage container create -n &lt;storage container name&gt; --account-name &lt;storage account name&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>az storage container create -n &lt;storage container name&gt; --account-name &lt;storage account name&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">This script will commit and push the corresponding YAML template into your repository, so please be sure your local repository is up-to-date (i.e you have pulled the latest changes with <code>git pull</code>).</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Creating the workflow using provided script</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Before executing the script you will need to customize some input variables about the environment. To do so, you can either edit <code>terraform.tfvars</code> file or take advantage of the <code>set-terraform-variables.sh</code> script located at <code>/scripts/environment-provisioning/azure/aks</code>, which allows you to create or update values for the required variables, passing them as flags. As a full example:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./set-terraform-variables.sh --location &lt;location&gt; --resource_group_name &lt;resource group name&gt; --instance_type &lt;worker instance type&gt; --worker_node_count &lt;number of worker nodes&gt; --dns_prefix &lt;dns prefix&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./set-terraform-variables.sh --location &lt;location&gt; --resource_group_name &lt;resource group name&gt; --instance_type &lt;worker instance type&gt; --worker_node_count &lt;number of worker nodes&gt; --dns_prefix &lt;dns prefix&gt;</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-usage" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Usage</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pipeline_generator.sh \
  -c &lt;config file path&gt; \

  [--rancher] \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]"><pre class="notranslate"><code>pipeline_generator.sh \

  -d &lt;project local path&gt; \

  --storage-container &lt;storage container name&gt; \
  [--rancher] \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<table>

</td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-flags" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-flags" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#flags"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Flags</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="-c, --config-file        [Required] Configuration file containing pipeline definition.
-n, --pipeline-name      [Required] Name that will be set to the pipeline.
-d, --local-directory    [Required] Local directory of your project (the path should always be using '/' and not '\').
    --cluster-name       [Required] Name for the cluster.
    --resource-group     [Required] Name of the resource group for the cluster.
    --storage--account   [Required] Name of the storage account for the cluster.
    --storage-container  [Required] Name of the storage container where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
    --rancher                       Install Rancher to manage the cluster.
-b, --target-branch                 Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                  Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag."><pre class="notranslate"><code>-c, --config-file        [Required] Configuration file containing pipeline definition.
-n, --pipeline-name      [Required] Name that will be set to the pipeline.
-d, --local-directory    [Required] Local directory of your project (the path should always be using '/' and not '\').
    --cluster-name       [Required] Name for the cluster.
    --resource-group     [Required] Name of the resource group for the cluster.
    --storage--account   [Required] Name of the storage account for the cluster.
    --storage-container  [Required] Name of the storage container where the Terraform state of the cluster will be stored.
    --rancher                       Install Rancher to manage the cluster.
-b, --target-branch                 Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                  Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag.</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-example" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-example" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Example</h3>

<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#appendix-interacting-with-the-cluster"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Appendix: Interacting with the cluster</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<table>
<tbody><tr>
<td>
<div dir="auto">Note</div>
</td>
<td>
Make sure you have <a href="https://kubernetes.io/docs/tasks/tools/#kubectl" rel="nofollow">kubectl</a> installed.
</td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">In order to interact with your cluster you will need to download the artifact <code>kubeconfig</code> generated by the cluster provisioning workflow on the location it is expected by default (<code>~/.kube/config</code>) or either:</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# via environment variable (you can add this on your profile)
export KUBECONFIG=&lt;path to downloaded kubeconfig&gt;
kubectl &lt;command&gt;
via command-line flag

kubectl <command> --kubeconfig=<path to downloaded kubeconfig>"><pre class="notranslate"><code># via environment variable (you can add this on your profile) export KUBECONFIG=<path to downloaded kubeconfig> kubectl <command>

via command-line flag

        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-setting-up-a-deploy-pipeline-on-github" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#setting-up-a-deploy-pipeline-on-github"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Setting up a Deploy Pipeline on Github</h1>
<div id="user-content-preamble" dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">In this section we will create a deploy workflow on Github to deploy the project application on an already provisioned Kubernetes cluster. This pipeline will be configured in order to be triggered every time package workflow is executed successfully on a commit for <code>release/*</code> and <code>develop</code> branches, requiring manual launch for other branches but still enforcing that package workflow has passed. By default, it depends on the environment provisioning workflow being successfully run on beforehand and, depending on the Kubernetes provider, it consumes the artifact produced by that. It also consumes variable groups created by package and environment provisioning workflow.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The creation of the pipeline will follow the project workflow, so a new branch named <code>feature/deploy-pipeline</code> will be created and the YAML file for the pipeline will be pushed to it.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">Then, a Pull Request (PR) will be created in order to merge the new branch into the appropriate branch (provided in <code>-b</code> flag). The PR will be automatically merged if the repository policies are met. If the merge is not possible, either the PR URL will be shown as output, or it will be opened in your web browser if using <code>-w</code> flag.</p>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<p dir="auto">The script located at <code>/scripts/pipelines/github/pipeline_generator.sh</code> will automatically create the new branch, create a deploy pipeline based on a YAML template appropriate for the project manifests files, create the Pull Request, and if it is possible, merge this new branch into the specified branch.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-prerequisites" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prerequisites</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">This script will commit and push the corresponding YAML template into your repository, so please be sure your local repository is up-to-date (i.e you have pulled the latest changes with <code>git pull</code>).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The YAML containing Deployment object should be named <code>application-deployment.yaml</code> for allowing automated <code>imagePullSecret</code> injection.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h2 id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#creating-the-workflow-using-provided-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Creating the workflow using provided script</h2>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-usage" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Usage</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pipeline_generator.sh \
  -c &lt;config file path&gt; \
  -n &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  -d &lt;project local path&gt; \
  --package-pipeline-name &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  --env-provision-pipeline-name &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  --k8s-provider &lt;provider name&gt; \
  --k8s-namespace &lt;namespace&gt; \
  --k8s-deploy-files-path &lt;manifests path&gt; \
  [--k8s-image-pull-secret-name &lt;secret name&gt;] \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]"><pre class="notranslate"><code>pipeline_generator.sh \
  -c &lt;config file path&gt; \
  -n &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  -d &lt;project local path&gt; \
  --package-pipeline-name &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  --env-provision-pipeline-name &lt;pipeline name&gt; \
  --k8s-provider &lt;provider name&gt; \
  --k8s-namespace &lt;namespace&gt; \
  --k8s-deploy-files-path &lt;manifests path&gt; \
  [--k8s-image-pull-secret-name &lt;secret name&gt;] \
  [-b &lt;branch&gt;] \
  [-w]</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<table>
<tbody><tr>
<td>
<div dir="auto">Note</div>
</td>
<td>
The config file for the deploy pipeline is located at <code>/scripts/pipelines/github/templates/deploy/deploy-pipeline.cfg</code>.
</td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-flags" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-flags" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#flags"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Flags</h3>
<div dir="auto">
<div dir="auto">
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="-c  --config-file                   [Required] Configuration file containing pipeline definition.
-n  --pipeline-name                 [Required] Name that will be set to the pipeline.
-d  --local-directory               [Required] Local directory of your project.
    --package-pipeline-name         [Required] Package pipeline name.
    --env-provision-pipeline-name   [Required] Environment provisioning pipeline name.
    --k8s-provider                  [Required] Kubernetes cluster provider name. Accepted values: EKS, AKS.
    --k8s-namespace                 [Required] Kubernetes namespace where the application will be deployed.
    --k8s-deploy-files-path         [Required] Path from the root of the project to the YAML manifests directory.
    --k8s-image-pull-secret-name    Name for the generated secret containing registry credentials. Required when using a private registry to host images.
-b  --target-branch                            Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                             Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag."><pre class="notranslate"><code>-c  --config-file                   [Required] Configuration file containing pipeline definition.
-n  --pipeline-name                 [Required] Name that will be set to the pipeline.
-d  --local-directory               [Required] Local directory of your project.
    --package-pipeline-name         [Required] Package pipeline name.
    --env-provision-pipeline-name   [Required] Environment provisioning pipeline name.
    --k8s-provider                  [Required] Kubernetes cluster provider name. Accepted values: EKS, AKS.
    --k8s-namespace                 [Required] Kubernetes namespace where the application will be deployed.
    --k8s-deploy-files-path         [Required] Path from the root of the project to the YAML manifests directory.
    --k8s-image-pull-secret-name    Name for the generated secret containing registry credentials. Required when using a private registry to host images.
-b  --target-branch                            Name of the branch to which the Pull Request will target. PR is not created if the flag is not provided.
-w                                             Open the Pull Request on the web browser if it cannot be automatically merged. Requires -b flag.</code></pre></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div dir="auto">
<h3 id="user-content-examples" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Examples</h3>
